 sakasacio

aRniSnavs, rom paSikovis mier Cadenili danaSauli _ narkomania warmoadgens

aRniSnulidan gamomdinare, sakasacio saCivari miiCnevs, rom paSikovisaTvis

motiviT.

ra saqmis masalebi, sakasacio saCivris motivTa


safuZvlianoba, moismina saqarTvelos generaluri prokuroris TanaSemwis m.

mivida im daskvnamde, rom ganaCeni paSikovis mimarT kanonieria 


da unda darCes 


ucvlelad Semdeg garemoebaTa gaTvaliswinebiT.


sasamarTlo kolegiam paSikovis mimarT sasjelis gansazRvris dros


gaiTvalswina rogorc mis mier Cadenili danaSauli sazogadoebrivad saSiSi


xasiaTi da xarisxi, aseve, damnaSavis pirovneba, misi pasuxis


mgeblobis 


Semamsubuqebeli garemoebebi. saxeldobr is, rom paSikovi samarTalSi pirveladaa, 


aRiarebs da inaniebs Cadenil danaSauls, kmayofaze hyavs meuRle da ori


arasrulwlovani Svili, moxuci mSoblebi, xasiaTdeba dadebiTad. aRsaniSnavia


isic, rom paSikovi pati


mrobaSi imyofeboda 6 Tve.
